  <raw>Porsche Officially Registers VW Takeover Plan with EU




Porsche has confirmed that it has registered its plan to gain a majority shareholding in the Volkswagen (VW) Group with the European Commission (EC) according to theFinancial Times Deutschland. The European Union (EU) competition authorities have already said that they are likely to reach a decision by 18 June on whether Porsche buying into VW will create a monopoly in the German automotive industry.

Significance:Porsche's statement is part of the legal procedure in its bid to gain a majority shareholding in Europe's largest volume carmaker. Porsche is planning to increase its stake in VW from around 30.8% to more than 50% as soon as the EC and 15 further anti-trust authorities give the acquisition the green light. It is confident that it will be free to acquire a majority stake later this year. Porsche is going ahead with acquiring a majority shareholding despite the fact that there is still some uncertainty over the German government's drafting of a new VW Law attempting to retain the controversial blocking minority, which could thwart Porsche's managerial control of VW.</raw>
